    "body": "Comment on cases 194-204.  I have interpreted all of these as NO CHANGE.  Many of these appear in\r\nMW or PW,PWG with the NKy replaced by NK.  This is a difficult ligature:\r\n![image](https://cloud.githubusercontent.com/assets/6393033/7598296/69da5f74-f8c7-11e4-87c6-6ec37eda93b0.png)\r\n\r\n@drdhaval2785 or @Shalu411  needs to check that this Devanagari ligature is  NKy   , as the Sanskrit typists and I think. \r\n\r\nIf this is NKy in ACC, I wonder if there is some reason other dictionaries have the NK spelling?\r\n\r\nHere are these cases:\r\n<hr/>\r\n194 SaNKyacakraDAraRavAda\r\n194 SaNKyacakraviDi ->  NO CHANGE:NKy difficult ligature.
